  <script>
   window.activeReg = 0;
        function switchMap(obj, value) {
            if (window.activeReg != obj.getAttribute('data-reg')) {
                document.all.div_map.getElementsByTagName('img')[obj.getAttribute('image_id') - 1].style.visibility = value;
                obj.blur();
            }
        }
        function activeRegion(obj) {
            $('.panel.regions').slideUp(500);
            $('.select-region .result-region p').text('');
            if (window.activeReg != obj.getAttribute('data-reg')) {
                $('.panel.region' + obj.getAttribute('data-reg')).slideDown(500);
                $('.select-region .result-region p').text($('.panel.region' + obj.getAttribute('data-reg') + ' .panel-title p').text());

                document.all.div_map.getElementsByTagName('img')[$('map#regions_map > area[data-reg="' + window.activeReg + '"]').attr('image_id') - 1].style.visibility = 'hidden';
                document.all.div_map.getElementsByTagName('img')[obj.getAttribute('image_id') - 1].style.visibility = 'visible';

                window.activeReg = obj.getAttribute('data-reg');
            } else {
                window.activeReg = 0;
            }
        }
        $('.select-mobi-refions').on('change',function(e){
            console.log('.mobi-region' + $(e.currentTarget).val());
            $('.regions-mobi').hide(200);
            $('.mobi-region' + $(e.currentTarget).val()).show(400);
        });
  </script>
  <script>
   $('form.developer-form').on('submit',function(e){
            $.ajax({
                type: "POST",
                url: '/form/developer',
                data: $(e.currentTarget).serialize(),
                success: function(d){console.log(d);$('.email-developer .close').click()}
            });
            return false;
        });
  </script>
